//===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\n8: //\n9: // This pass inserts stack protectors into functions which need them. A variable\n10: // with a random value in it is stored onto the stack before the local variables\n11: // are allocated. Upon exiting the block, the stored value is checked. class SSPLayoutAnalysis;\n37:   friend class StackProtector;\n38:   static constexpr unsigned DefaultSSPBufferSize = 8;\n39: \n40:   /// A mapping of AllocaInsts to their required SSP layout.\n41:   using SSPLayoutMap =\n42:       DenseMap<const AllocaInst *, MachineFrameInfo::SSPLayoutKind>;\n43: \n44:   /// Layout - Mapping of allocations to the required SSPLayoutKind.\n45:   /// StackProtector generated.\n56:   bool HasPrologue = false;\n57: \n58:   // IR checking code is generated.\n59:   bool HasIRCheck = false;\n60: \n61: public:\n62:   // Return true if StackProtector is supposed to be handled by SelectionDAG.\n63:   bool shouldEmitSDCheck(const BasicBlock &BB) const;\n64: \n65:   void copyToMachineFrameInfo(MachineFrameInfo &MFI) const;\n66: };\n67: \n68: class SSPLayoutAnalysis : public AnalysisInfoMixin<SSPLayoutAnalysis> {\n69:   friend AnalysisInfoMixin<SSPLayoutAnalysis>;\n70:   using SSPLayoutMap = SSPLayoutInfo::SSPLayoutMap;\n71: \n72:   static AnalysisKey Key;\n73: StackProtector();\n111: \n112:   SSPLayoutInfo &getLayoutInfo() { return LayoutInfo; }\n113: \n114:   void getAnalysisUsage(AnalysisUsage &AU) const override;\n115: \n116:   // Return true if \"llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/BoundsChecking.cpp\",\n      \"symbol\": \"addBoundsChecking\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"Stack protection mechanisms in LLVM are implemented across multiple components that work together to detect and prevent stack buffer overflow attacks:\\n\\n## 1. Stack Protector Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/StackProtector.cpp)\\nThe main LLVM pass that inserts stack protectors into functions. The `StackProtector` class is a `FunctionPass` that:\\n- Detects functions requiring stack protection based on -fstack-protector flags\\n- Inserts stack guard values before local variables\\n- Inserts verification checks in epilogues that call `__stack_chk_fail()` if corruption is detected\\n- Key function: `InsertStackProtectors()` - implements prologue/epilogue insertion logic\\n- Key function: `CreateFailBB()` - creates the failure basic block with call to __stack_chk_fail\\n\\n## 2. Stack Protector Interface (llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/StackProtector.h)\\nDefines the public interface for stack protection:\\n- `StackProtectorPass` - Modern pass interface using PassManager\\n- `StackProtector` - Legacy FunctionPass interface\\n- `SSPLayoutAnalysis` - Analyzes which variables trigger stack protection requirements\\n- `SSPLayoutInfo` - Stores layout information for protected stack objects\\n\\n## 3. SafeStack Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStack.cpp)\\nImplements the SafeStack security feature that partitions the stack into safe and unsafe regions:\\n- `SafeStack` class - main implementation for separating stack allocations\\n- `SafeStackLegacyPass` - legacy pass interface\\n- Separates allocations that are proven safe from those that could be vulnerable\\n- Unsafe allocations are moved to dynamically allocated unsafe stack managed by runtime library\\n- Includes stack protector checks for unsafe stack allocations\\n\\n## 4. SafeStack Interface (llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/SafeStack.h)\\nDeclarates the public interface:\\n- `SafeStackPass` - Modern new-PM compatible pass interface\\n- Processes functions with SafeStack attribute\\n\\n## 5. SafeStack Layout (llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStackLayout.cpp/h)\\nManages frame layout for safe and unsafe stacks:\\n- `StackLayout` class - organizes stack objects with coloring and alignment\\n- `layoutObject()` - places stack objects efficiently in memory\\n- `addObject()` - registers new stack objects\\n- Ensures proper separation and alignment of stack allocations\\n\\n## 6. Stack Check Failure Handler (libc/src/compiler/generic/__stack_chk_fail.cpp)\\nRuntime implementation of the stack protection library function:\\n- `__stack_chk_fail()` - called when stack corruption is detected, prints \\\"stack smashing detected\\\\n\\\" and aborts\\n- `__stack_chk_guard` - global variable containing the random guard value (initialized to 0xa9fff01234)\\n- Located in LLVM libc's compiler support library\\n\\n## 7. Bounds Checking Instrumentation (llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/BoundsChecking.cpp)\\nProvides additional memory safety instrumentation for bounds checking:\\n- `BoundsCheckingPass` - detects and instruments out-of-bounds memory access operations\\n- `getBoundsCheckCond()` - determines conditions under which memory access will overflow\\n- `addBoundsChecking()` - inserts checks before load/store instructions\\n- Complements stack protectors with checks for heap and other memory regions\\n- Header at llvm/include/llvm/Transforms/Instrumentation/BoundsChecking.h\\n\\nTogether, these components provide defense-in-depth against stack buffer overflow attacks: StackProtector adds canary checks, SafeStack separates unsafe allocations to protected memory, and BoundsChecking instruments memory accesses to detect violations at runtime.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3411,"cache_read_input_tokens":78805,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3411},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"b487a06a-02bb-4ca6-bdbb-e942bb5f7cf2","uuid":"9e4928bd-16e3-4ce9-b366-839bc56be084"}

components that work together to detect and prevent stack buffer overflow attacks:\\n\\n## 1. Stack Protector Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/StackProtector.cpp)\\nThe main LLVM pass that inserts stack protectors into functions. The `StackProtector` class is a `FunctionPass` that:\\n- Detects functions requiring stack protection based on -fstack-protector flags\\n- Inserts stack guard values before local variables\\n- Inserts verification checks in epilogues that call `__stack_chk_fail()` if corruption is detected\\n- Key function: `InsertStackProtectors()` - implements prologue/epilogue insertion logic\\n- Key function: `CreateFailBB()` - creates the failure basic block with call to __stack_chk_fail\\n\\n## 2. Stack Protector Interface (llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/StackProtector.h)\\nDefines the public interface for stack protection:\\n- `StackProtectorPass` - Modern pass interface using PassManager\\n- `StackProtector` - Legacy FunctionPass interface\\n- `SSPLayoutAnalysis` - Analyzes which variables trigger stack protection requirements\\n- `SSPLayoutInfo` - Stores layout information for protected stack objects\\n\\n## 3. SafeStack Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStack.cpp)\\nImplements the SafeStack security feature that partitions the stack into safe and unsafe regions:\\n- `SafeStack` class - main implementation for separating stack allocations\\n- `SafeStackLegacyPass` - legacy pass interface\\n- Separates allocations that are proven safe from those that could be vulnerable\\n- Unsafe allocations are moved to dynamically allocated unsafe stack managed by runtime library\\n- Includes stack protector checks for unsafe stack allocations\\n\\n## 4. SafeStack Interface (llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/SafeStack.h)\\nDeclarates the public interface:\\n- `SafeStackPass` - Modern new-PM compatible pass interface\\n- Processes functions with SafeStack attribute\\n\\n## 5. SafeStack Layout (llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStackLayout.cpp/h)\\nManages frame layout for safe and unsafe stacks:\\n- `StackLayout` class - organizes stack objects with coloring and alignment\\n- `layoutObject()` - places stack objects efficiently in memory\\n- `addObject()` - registers new stack objects\\n- Ensures proper separation and alignment of stack allocations\\n\\n## 6. Stack Check Failure Handler (libc/src/compiler/generic/__stack_chk_fail.cpp)\\nRuntime implementation of the stack protection library function:\\n- `__stack_chk_fail()` - called when stack corruption is detected, prints \\\"stack smashing detected\\\\n\\\" and aborts\\n- `__stack_chk_guard` - global variable containing the random guard value (initialized to 0xa9fff01234)\\n- Located in LLVM libc's compiler support library\\n\\n## 7. Bounds Checking Instrumentation (llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/BoundsChecking.cpp)\\nProvides additional memory safety instrumentation for bounds checking:\\n- `BoundsCheckingPass` - detects and instruments out-of-bounds memory access operations\\n- `getBoundsCheckCond()` - determines conditions under which memory access will overflow\\n- `addBoundsChecking()` - inserts checks before load/store instructions\\n- Complements stack protectors with checks for heap and other memory regions\\n- Header at llvm/include/llvm/Transforms/Instrumentation/BoundsChecking.h\\n\\nTogether, these components provide defense-in-depth against stack buffer overflow attacks: StackProtector adds canary checks, SafeStack separates unsafe allocations to protected memory, and BoundsChecking instruments memory accesses to detect violations at runtime.\"\n}\n","numLines":119,"startLine":1,"totalLines":119}}}
